				<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading pagetitle page-header">
					Gleichwie der Regen und Schnee vom Himmel fällt, BWV 18 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)				</h1>	

				<div class="body"><div lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr"><div class="wp_header">
<table>
<table>

<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>5 sections
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composition Year
</th>
<td>1713-14, revised 1724
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Genre Categories<span class="addpagetag mh555"></span>

<h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="General_Information">General Information</span></h2>
<div class="wi_body" style="width:100%">
<table border="0">

<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Work Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head" style="width:100%">Gleichwie der Regen und Schnee vom Himmel fällt
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Alt<span class="mh555">ernative</span><span class="ms555">.</span> Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head">Just like the rain and snow falling from the heavens
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Name Translations
</th>
<td><span title="he">Gleichwie der Regen und Schnee vom Himmel fällt, רי"ב 18</span>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Authorities
</th>
<td><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.worldcat.org/identities/containsVIAFID/177884880">WorldCat</a>; <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gleichwie_der_Regen_und_Schnee_vom_Himmel_f%C3%A4llt,_BWV_18">Wikipedia</a>; <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Virtual_International_Authority_File" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Virtual International Authority File">VIAF</a>: <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://viaf.org/viaf/177884880">177884880</a>; <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Biblioth%C3%A8que_nationale_de_France" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Bibliothèque nationale de France">BNF</a>: <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://catalogue.bnf.fr/ark:/12148/cb13909533n">13909533n</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composer
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Bach,_Johann_Sebastian" title="Category:Bach, Johann Sebastian">Bach, Johann Sebastian</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Opus/Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">Op./Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td>BWV 18
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">I-Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">I-Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td>IJB 247
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Key
</th>
<td>G minor (Weimer version)<br />A minor (Leipzig version)
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>5 sections:
<ol><li>Sinfonia
</li><li>Recitativo (soprano): Gleichwie der Regen und Schnee vom Himmel fällt
</li><li>Recitativo &amp; Chorale (tenor, bass): Mein Gott, hier wird mein Herze sein
</li><li>Aria (soprano): Mein Seelenschatz ist Gottes Wort
</li><li>Chorale: Ich bitt, o Herr, aus Herzens Grund
</li></ol>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Year/Date of Composition</span><span class="ms555">Y/D of Comp.</span>
</th>
<td>1713-14, revised 1724
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>First Perf<span class="mh555">ormance</span><span class="ms555">.</span>
</th>
<td>1713/1715 in Weimar<br />1724-02-13 (after the Sermon) Nikolaikirche Leipzig
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>First Pub<span class="mh555">lication</span><span class="ms555">.</span>
</th>
<td>1852 (BGA)
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Librettist
</th>
<td><i>see below</i>
<dl><dd>Isaiah 55: 10-12 (No.2)<br /><a href="/wiki/Category:Neumeister,_Erdmann" title="Category:Neumeister, Erdmann">Erdmann Neumeister</a> (1671-1756) (Nos.3-4)<br /><a href="/wiki/Category:Spengler,_Lazarus" title="Category:Spengler, Lazarus">Lazarus Spengler</a> (1479-1534) (No.5)
</dd></dl>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Language
</th>
<td>German
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Dedication
</th>
<td>Sexagesima Sunday
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Average Duration</span><span class="ms555">Avg. Duration</span>
</th>
<td>21 minutes
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Composer Time Period</span><span class="ms555">Comp. Period</span>
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Baroque" title="Category:Baroque">Baroque</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Piece Style
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Baroque_style" title="Category:Baroque style">Baroque</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Instrumentation
</th>
<td><i>Voices:</i> soprano, tenor, bass; mixed chorus (SATB)<br /><i>Orchestra:</i> 2 recorders (none in Weimar), bassoon, 4 violas, cello, continuo
</td></tr>

<td style="background-color: #e6f0f5">
<ul><li>I. Jauchzet, frohlocket, auf, preiset die Tage

</li><li>III. Herrscher des Himmels, erhöre das Lallen
</li><li>IV. Fallt mit Danken, fallt mit Loben
</li><li>V. Ehre sei dir, Gott, gesungen
</li><li>VI. Herr, wenn die stolzen Feinde schnauben
